 jQuery( ".sticky-popup" ).css( "visibility", "visible" );

 jQuery('.sticky-popup').addClass("popup-content-bounce-in-right");

 if(jQuery('.sticky-popup').hasClass("open"))
 {

 }
 else
 {

 jQuery( ".sticky-popup" ).css( "right", 0 );
